<div id="review_2360715430" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2360715430" />
    <a title="Hollis " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16668577-hollis"><img alt="Hollis " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586714618p2/16668577.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2360715430?book_show_action=true">Apr 13, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hollis " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hollis " href="/user/show/16668577-hollis">Hollis </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=all-the-feels">all-the-feels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=all-the-lols">all-the-lols</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=alphamales-i-want">alphamales-i-want</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=buddy-read-sorta">buddy-read-sorta</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=hello-diversity">hello-diversity</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=2018-reads">2018-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=heroes-to-root-for">heroes-to-root-for</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=hist-romance">hist-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2360715430" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer254700494060576309">This review can also be found at <a href='http://www.romantichistoricalreviews.com/retro-review-seduce-me-at-sunrise-the-hathaways-2-by-lisa-kleypas/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Romantic Historical Reviews</a>.<br/><br/>Being relatively new to the historical romance genre, and thus totally overwhelmed by the selection and substantial backlists of all the Must Read Authors, it's taken a few years for me to get caught up on some of the books that are absolute staples and longtime favourites of so many readers. Which is why you see so many ‘retro reviews’ with my name on them! Naturally, many of those favorites come from the pen of Lisa Kleypas. I devour</span>
  <span id="freeText254700494060576309" style="display:none">This review can also be found at <a href="http://www.romantichistoricalreviews.com/retro-review-seduce-me-at-sunrise-the-hathaways-2-by-lisa-kleypas/" rel="nofollow noopener">Romantic Historical Reviews</a>.<br /><br />Being relatively new to the historical romance genre, and thus totally overwhelmed by the selection and substantial backlists of all the Must Read Authors, it's taken a few years for me to get caught up on some of the books that are absolute staples and longtime favourites of so many readers. Which is why you see so many ‘retro reviews’ with my name on them! Naturally, many of those favorites come from the pen of Lisa Kleypas. I devoured her <i>
  <b>Wallflowers</b>
</i> series back in 2016 and promised myself a more leisurely pace for future spinoff series, wanting to savour them, even though I had so many to catch up on. Which brings us to 2018 and my journey through <i>
  <b>The Hathaways </b>
</i> series.<br /><br /><b>Seduce Me at Sunrise</b> is actually the second installment and though I read the first one – <b>Mine Till Midnight</b> – a few months ago, I was thrown right back into the thick of things with this family. And that's where this series shines: the Hathaway siblings.<br /><br />With four sisters and their brother, the Hathaway children had a somewhat irregular upbringing as their family was fond of debate and discussion and were both accepting and liberal as well as scholarly. So liberal, in fact, that after discovering a young Romany boy left for dead near their property, their father ensured that not only was he nursed back to health but he was also allowed to stay to live and be part of their family. Not quite a ward, not quite a servant, but somewhere in between; much like how he was both Gypsy and tribeless, cast out, and caught between two worlds.<br /><br />Young, mistreated, and prone to lashing out, Merripen nonetheless finds himself powerfully drawn to Winnifred, second eldest daughter, and as the years pass his love for her only grows stronger. After the death of their parents, the Hathaways have a further string of misfortune when scarlet fever lays both Win and her brother Leo low, almost killing them, and the event leaves Win forever frail with compromised lung capacity. Merripen is devoted to her, careful with her, protective, but after years of being treated like glass, when she confronts him with her feelings for him, and he cannot return them because he feels so unworthy of her (not that he tells her this, of course), she decides she will no longer be trapped by her illness and goes to France to seek a cure.<br /><br />Two years later and Winnifred has her health, a suitor in the form of the doctor who has returned to England with her to court her, and still Merripen resists their connection even in the face of competition and Winnifred's improved state. He pushes and pulls her, unable to resist, lashing out when he gives in to her, and the back and forth is both frustrating and yet redeemed by Kleypas having Winnifred acknowledge the situation instead of just being swept along by the man's behaviour, like so many HR heroines often are. And while I occasionally fluttered at Merripen's epic intense love that still made it impossible for him to be with her – which is where my flutters turned to aggravated flails – the real strength of the story is in the family and secondary characters.<br /><br />We have a shifting POV in <b>Seduce Me at Sunrise</b>; Cam – book one's hero, who happens to be another gypsy with an unusual connection to Merripen, has a part to play, and we are also blessed with Leo's POV. Both men are full of witty, hilarious, charming dialogue and observations, and combined they are an absolute delight. The whole family is, really, but these two really had me going at times. And the total sweetness of seeing the tender moments between Cam and Amelia after their heard-earned HEA in <b>Mine Till Midnight</b> were just.. gah, feels. Additional feels were provided by the appearance of characters the <i>
  <b>Wallflowers</b>
</i> series; I so loved seeing Simon and Annabelle again and hope the author continues to sprinkle previous couples throughout the upcoming books.<br /><br />Kleypas has always balanced angst with humour, and kept the emotional current strong despite that, and this story is no different. I really did love Win and Merripen together.. but only when they were together (and whew, were they ever hot together, too, my goodness!) Merripen gives the stack of broody heroes I've loved in the past a run for their money with how tightly he suppresses everything, made worse by the intensity with which he feels it all, and that was hard to read. I really enjoyed the lighter moments during the first half, though, which made it much easier to bear. But Win is strong, she's no doormat of a heroine, and that helped, too.<br /><br />I also loved how the author takes time to really explore the Romany culture and make that a relevant feature, not just window dressing, and it definitely plays a strong part in this book with one, two, maybe even three surprising revelations along the way.<br /><br />This second book in this much-loved series was very enjoyable and there is so much plot laid for the remaining siblings that it's impossible not to want to dive right into book three. If you haven't read this series yet, but haven't read the <i>
  <b>Wallflowers</b>
</i> yet either, then don’t! Start with the <i>
  <b>Wallflowers</b>
</i> and then make your way to <i>The Hathaways</i>. You won't regret it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="254700494060576309" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText5625407447376543533" style="display:none"><br><br>My Least Favorite Love Story In This Series<br><br>Merripen Is Grumpy (Not A Fan Of An Angry Hero)<br><br>A Love Triangle (Not A Fan)<br><br>BUUUUTTT It Has These Wonderful Moments From The Hathaway's<br><br><br><b>“To Cam surprise, she was smiling up at him steadily, her eyes midnight.<br>His expression turned quizzical. <span id="freeTextContainer14151945728872978782">Rating: 4 stars<br/><br/><b>Seduce Me at Sunrise</b> started out fierce. Then the plot got a little lumpy like an old mattress in the middle (comfortable but overused), and then bounced up and down again with a few plot twists at the end. Lisa Kleypas knows her stuff. She redeemed the story and mellowed my frustration. <br/><br/>Merripen's intensity and darkness kept the plot fires going, along with his strong passion for Winnifred. Another turn that proved positive was Win is revealed to have very human flaws. She is mor</span>
  <span id="freeText14151945728872978782" style="display:none">Rating: 4 stars<br /><br /><b>Seduce Me at Sunrise</b> started out fierce. Then the plot got a little lumpy like an old mattress in the middle (comfortable but overused), and then bounced up and down again with a few plot twists at the end. Lisa Kleypas knows her stuff. She redeemed the story and mellowed my frustration. <br /><br />Merripen's intensity and darkness kept the plot fires going, along with his strong passion for Winnifred. Another turn that proved positive was Win is revealed to have very human flaws. She is more than a match for him. I didn't care for how she was portrayed earlier as this ethereal flawless creature too good to be on earth.<br /><br />My favorite couple of the series, Cam and Amelia, are adorable. The new governess, Miss Marks and Leo don't interest me as much. Out of all the books, I'm not certain I will be reading their story. Beatrix and Poppy are fun, sweet and smart, displaying hints of girlish mischief still. I can't wait to see how Poppy reaches her HEA.<br /><br />I'm looking forward to the next book, regretting that I read Beatrix's story first. I was fast-forwarded into the future of what happens with everyone later. It's a mistake I won't make again. </span>
  <a data-text-id="14151945728872978782" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2104932888" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2104932888" />
    <a title="Jan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/57282794-jan"><img alt="Jan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505016022p2/57282794.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2104932888?book_show_action=true">Aug 27, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jan" href="/user/show/57282794-jan">Jan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57282794-jan?shelf=historical">historical</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57282794-jan?shelf=victorian-era">victorian-era</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2104932888" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13597676161441783149">Hah! Really enjoyed this second book about the Hathaway family. I'm really starting to like this interesting and convincingly portrayed family. Each of the siblings is unique and engaging, and I can't wait to read all of their stories!<br/><br/>This one focuses on the gypsy Kev Merripen, who was abandoned as a child and raised in the loving and slightly eccentric Hathaway household. He is now a kind of a trusted brother to them, and kind of a servant/ man-of-all-work. But since the Hathaways' house burned</span>
  <span id="freeText13597676161441783149" style="display:none">Hah! Really enjoyed this second book about the Hathaway family. I'm really starting to like this interesting and convincingly portrayed family. Each of the siblings is unique and engaging, and I can't wait to read all of their stories!<br /><br />This one focuses on the gypsy Kev Merripen, who was abandoned as a child and raised in the loving and slightly eccentric Hathaway household. He is now a kind of a trusted brother to them, and kind of a servant/ man-of-all-work. But since the Hathaways' house burned down (no spoiler cos it happened in the previous novel!) Kev has stepped up and shown his superb organisational skills in managing the vast rebuild project.<br /><br />Ever since the young boy Kev arrived in their household, there had been a special connection and friendship between him and the second daughter Win. Win had almost died a couple of years ago from an illness that left her with weak lungs. She goes to a clinic in France for treatment, and is away for quite period of time. She is finally well again when she returns - the treatment was successful. But she has also brought her doctor back to England with her, and there is a budding romance between the two of them. Kev is jealous and frustrated, because no matter how much he wants Win for himself, a part of him keeps refusing her. His difficult childhood (pre-Hathaways) has formed him into a highly passionate and quick-tempered person, but he fears he is too uncouth and violent for the sweet Win.<br /><br />So, the plot proceeds. It's not an easy path for Kev and Win toward their HEA. Several dramatic incidents occur, and it takes time for them, especially Kev, to accept that they will be together. <br /><br />The story also involves other family members, and the history of Kev's family background is eventually made known. <br /><br />We meet a new character in this book, the girls' prim governess Ms Marks, whom Leo Hathaway loathes but is oddly attracted to. Hmmmm..... :D And there is a crucial role in the story played by Beatrix Hathaway's cute pet ferret!<br /><br />Overall, I was carried along by the story in a most enjoyable way, and I look forward to the other books in the series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13597676161441783149" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_45268093" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/45268093" />
    <a title="Dina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1918270-dina"><img alt="Dina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460302951p2/1918270.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/45268093?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dina" href="/user/show/1918270-dina">Dina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1918270-dina?shelf=to-blog">to-blog</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1918270-dina?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer45268093&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer45268093" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18325825262337687774">After being seriously disappointed with <b>Mine Till Midnight</b>, the 1st book in this series, I´m happy to see things get back on track with <b>Seduce Me at Sunrise</b>. :)<br/><br/>I loved Merripen since he was introduced in the previous book and, thankfully, I still love him after reading his own book. He was tortured, brooding and fierce, just the way I like it. ;) He could have been less stubborn and I almost hated him when he didn´t rise to defend Win´s honor at the Hunt´s ball, but I easily "forgave" him for th</span>
  <span id="freeText18325825262337687774" style="display:none">After being seriously disappointed with <b>Mine Till Midnight</b>, the 1st book in this series, I´m happy to see things get back on track with <b>Seduce Me at Sunrise</b>. :)<br /><br />I loved Merripen since he was introduced in the previous book and, thankfully, I still love him after reading his own book. He was tortured, brooding and fierce, just the way I like it. ;) He could have been less stubborn and I almost hated him when he didn´t rise to defend Win´s honor at the Hunt´s ball, but I easily "forgave" him for that when he "broke down" later and literally swept her away.<br /><br />It was nice to see Win strong and free of all that "frail and angelic air" that surrounded her in <b>Mine Till Midnight</b>. She knew what she wanted, went for it and wasn´t going to conform and accept less than what she deserved.<br /><br />As in the previous book, there were several scenes involving the other members of the Hathaway family aside from Merripen and Win, but that didn´t annoy me this time - probably because Kleypas did a better job convincing me that Merripen and Win were really "connected", so I didn´t feel the need to see them <i>all the time</i>. Speaking of the secondary characters, it was very nice to see Leo "redeemed" from his previous actions. I can´t say how much I <i>hated</i> him in <b>Mine Till Midnight</b>, ugh, but my feelings towards him made a complete U-turn when he delivered that little speech that finally put some sense into Merripen´s mind.<br /><br />The only thing I didn´t like about this book was the "twist" that Kleypas did with Merripen´s origins. Okay, it was nice to have Cam as his brother - and I loved Cam´s "gentle" banter -, but was it necessary to make Merripen a titled <i>gadjo</i>? He never really cared about anything but Win - and vice versa - so it wasn´t as if they needed that to reach their HEA. It was too much, IMHO.<br /><br />All in all, I really enjoyed this book and the Hathaways are growing on me. I´ll definitely buy the next book in the series as soon as it´s released.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18325825262337687774" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_146704402" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/146704402" />
    <a title="Andrea" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4784586-andrea"><img alt="Andrea" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1373481234p2/4784586.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/146704402?book_show_action=true">Feb 08, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Andrea" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Andrea" href="/user/show/4784586-andrea">Andrea</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4784586-andrea?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer146704402" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10452230315978279388">And the Hathaways-re-read-athon with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1310208194' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lacey</a> continues.<br/><br/>This is just sad. It proves that some favorites should not be revisited but instead remembered fondly. I loved this book the last time I read it (which, Goodreads tells me, was four years ago)! I gave it five stars! It was on my favorites shelf!<br/><br/>And yet...<br/><br/>Times change. You grow up and evolve, your tastes change. It's not the book's fault. But lately I've found out that I have become less and less tolerant when it comes to brooding "heroes" who </span>
  <span id="freeText10452230315978279388" style="display:none">And the Hathaways-re-read-athon with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1310208194" rel="nofollow noopener">Lacey</a> continues.<br /><br />This is just sad. It proves that some favorites should not be revisited but instead remembered fondly. I loved this book the last time I read it (which, Goodreads tells me, was four years ago)! I gave it five stars! It was on my favorites shelf!<br /><br />And yet...<br /><br />Times change. You grow up and evolve, your tastes change. It's not the book's fault. But lately I've found out that I have become less and less tolerant when it comes to brooding "heroes" who string their "heroines" along. What ruined this book for me this time around is pretty easily explained: I grew tired of Kev and his constant hot and cold treatment. Honestly, any woman deserves better than this, and I don't care if he has her "best intentions" at heart. If he thinks he is unworthy of her, that is not his call to make. It's hers. All he can do is accept that she knows what she wants and respect her wishes or stay.the.hell.away. But this continued "oh my love will kill the poor frail woman but I can't restrain myself" annoyed me to no end. It's not fair to her. And yes. He has issues. Bad childhood. He's an animal and she a delicate flower *rolls eyes* Get over it. But don't beat me over the head with it. Don't get the girl's hopes up only to publicly humiliate her and squash her hopes over and over again. <br /><br />And another thing. What is with the attempt at a love triangle? There were so many moment were I wished Win would just move on, but the poor thing never even had a chance. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The only other man interested in her turns out to be a villain. Seriously, why is it neither Amelia nor Win allowed to have a real alternative? Why did both men have to be evil? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Anyway. I liked this book for the glimpses of the other Hathaways. Leo has grown quite a bit since the last book, Beatrix's darling pet Dodger is a delight... <br /><br />Oh well. <br /><br />On to the next book!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10452230315978279388" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer14401411546617201012"><br/>3.5<br/>It was going so well... first off, if somehow Lisa Kleypas could've rearranged the storylines, the first would've worked better for me. This was so much richer and better in the family aspect. I have to admit, the family is the reason I'm liking the series so much better than the individual installments. <br/> <br/>This was undoubtedly sweet, and I thought the beginning was going to make this add up to a standout of hers for me. It was still really, really good, and I really liked Win, but the secondar</span>
  <span id="freeText14401411546617201012" style="display:none"><br />3.5<br />It was going so well... first off, if somehow Lisa Kleypas could've rearranged the storylines, the first would've worked better for me. This was so much richer and better in the family aspect. I have to admit, the family is the reason I'm liking the series so much better than the individual installments. <br /> <br />This was undoubtedly sweet, and I thought the beginning was going to make this add up to a standout of hers for me. It was still really, really good, and I really liked Win, but the secondary characters stole the show for me--particularly Cam and Leo. What a bummer. I love the carrying-a-flame / unrequited (or assumed unrequited) trope, but I tired quickly of the back and forth. And here's what kind of fell apart for me....<br /> <br />If Kev was so concerned for Win's safety and what was best for her, yet controlling, how could he ever trust another man to that? In the middle with all the Julian stuff, I really felt like his character felt too inconsistent and reluctant. He would absolutely never leave her to this. I also have trouble with the self-sacrificing, know-what's-best hero being ever so reluctant.  I did love how Win broke through to Kev and was the only one who could do it-this is the case with many of my favorite romances, I just didn't buy the middle part.<br /> <br />Luckily, it smoothed out for me at the end. The scenes with Cam in the field were vivid and really well done IMO. Oh, but one minor annoyance -- <br /> <br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />Does he have to be an heir. My goodness. <br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /> <br /> <br /> </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2002499988" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer6762713141793850838"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/>I didn’t want to read this series out of order, but I’ll take what I can get from the library. I’m on a binge Lisa Kleypas read and I’m going into The Hathaways series. <br/><br/>This is Kev and Win’s book.<br/><br/>This book is filled with ANGST! Gah, I don’t know how I survived, I was pulling my hair out from the first page.<br/><br/>Kev isn’t a gentlemen, but a gypsy. Different right? Win’s family adopted him when he was in the near brink of death. Because of Win, Kev stayed with the family.<br/><br/>I’m not sure how I fee</span>
  <span id="freeText6762713141793850838" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br /><br />I didn’t want to read this series out of order, but I’ll take what I can get from the library. I’m on a binge Lisa Kleypas read and I’m going into The Hathaways series. <br /><br />This is Kev and Win’s book.<br /><br />This book is filled with ANGST! Gah, I don’t know how I survived, I was pulling my hair out from the first page.<br /><br />Kev isn’t a gentlemen, but a gypsy. Different right? Win’s family adopted him when he was in the near brink of death. Because of Win, Kev stayed with the family.<br /><br />I’m not sure how I feel about Kev. At times I loved him because of his passion, his stubbornness and his feelings towards Win. It’s the can’t-breathe-out-of-this-world kind of love you know? BUT goodness he was stubborn! I wanted to punch him in the face several times. He simply didn’t feel like he was good enough for Win.<br /><br />Win went through a lot in this book. She was sick and went away for two years. You would think a two year difference would get Kev to do something towards Win, but nope, he just brooded and was a jerk. If you like a push and pull kind of relationship then this is your book because this couple will get you going. Going crazy!<br /><br />Overall, I love these historical romances and I’m moving on to the next one.</span>

<div id="review_30069646" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/30069646" />
    <a title="Julie (jjmachshev)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/882708-julie-jjmachshev"><img alt="Julie (jjmachshev)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1208126390p2/882708.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/30069646?book_show_action=true">Aug 13, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Julie (jjmachshev)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Julie (jjmachshev)" href="/user/show/882708-julie-jjmachshev">Julie (jjmachshev)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/882708-julie-jjmachshev?shelf=2008-reads">2008-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer30069646" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13193868827813014616">I still have a sappy smile on my face! "Seduce Me at Sunrise" is one of the best historical romances I've read this year starring one of the most tortured heroes. This 2nd book in Lisa Kleypas' 'Hathaways' series brings us the story of the wild Rom boy, Kev Merripen, and his journey to love with Winnifred Hathaway.<br/><br/>Winnifred has loved Kev since the day he came into her home when she was still a young child. Her understanding and care of the feral boy hasn't made living with this love any easier, </span>
  <span id="freeText13193868827813014616" style="display:none">I still have a sappy smile on my face! "Seduce Me at Sunrise" is one of the best historical romances I've read this year starring one of the most tortured heroes. This 2nd book in Lisa Kleypas' 'Hathaways' series brings us the story of the wild Rom boy, Kev Merripen, and his journey to love with Winnifred Hathaway.<br /><br />Winnifred has loved Kev since the day he came into her home when she was still a young child. Her understanding and care of the feral boy hasn't made living with this love any easier, though. When she is stricken with scarlet fever and never quite regains her health, she becomes even more determined to do whatever is necessary to have Kev for her own. So she heads for France and a controversial clinic, leaving behind an increasingly wild Kev.<br /><br />Kev has loved Winn since he 'felt' her presence in the gadjo house that became his home. As a gypsy orphan with no protector, he was raised as a wild animalistic fighter who knew no gentleness until the Hathaways rescued a sick boy left for dead. He's never allowed himself to feel a part of the family, but has acted as their personal protector, defender, servant, or whatever else was needed. He craves Winn but won't sully her with his fierce demands. But he can't quite let her go either.<br /><br />What a powerful love and what a splendid story. You will admire Winn's determination and sometimes want to thump Kev for his stubborness. But to have a love so strong...what wouldn't we be willing to suffer?<br /><br />Kleypas' books have been more hits than misses with me, but this is truly a book you shouldn't miss. The emotions will wring you out and the passion will set your heart racing. And at the end, you'll have the same sappy smile on your face!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13193868827813014616" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_185428377" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/185428377" />
    <a title="Ronyell" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1169488-ronyell"><img alt="Ronyell" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1506581787p2/1169488.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/185428377?book_show_action=true">Jul 16, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ronyell" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ronyell" href="/user/show/1169488-ronyell">Ronyell</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of Lisa Kleypas' works!!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=british-hero-or-heroine">british-hero-or-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=ronyell-s-epinions-reviews">ronyell-s-epinions-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=manners">manners</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=sexy-bad-boy-hero">sexy-bad-boy-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=sexy-good-girl-heroine">sexy-good-girl-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=adult-book">adult-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=aar-top-100-romance-books-2010">aar-top-100-romance-books-2010</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=english-books">english-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=lisa-kleypas">lisa-kleypas</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer185428377" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15222096595506976151">After reading all of Lisa Kleypas’ popular “Wallflower” series and reading her first book in the “Hathaway” series, “Mine Till Midnight,” I was definitely going to try my luck in reading the second book in the “Hathaway” series, “Seduce Me at Sunrise.” This second installment in the fantastic “Hathaway” is just as brilliant as the first book as it is full of forbidden secrets, an undying love and hot sizzling romance that will have you flipping over with anticipation!<br/><br/>Winnifred Hathaway was alway</span>
  <span id="freeText15222096595506976151" style="display:none">After reading all of Lisa Kleypas’ popular “Wallflower” series and reading her first book in the “Hathaway” series, “Mine Till Midnight,” I was definitely going to try my luck in reading the second book in the “Hathaway” series, “Seduce Me at Sunrise.” This second installment in the fantastic “Hathaway” is just as brilliant as the first book as it is full of forbidden secrets, an undying love and hot sizzling romance that will have you flipping over with anticipation!<br /><br />Winnifred Hathaway was always ill ever since she was affected by the scarlet fever years ago that nearly took her life. Now, Winnifred finally has the chance to get well again by going to a well-known clinic in France that is run by Dr. Julian Harrow and when she comes back home from her treatment, Winnifred has become a changed woman! Kev Merripen, the handsome and strong Romany Gypsy that the Hathaway family has taken in ever since he was a boy, has always loved Winnifred, but because of his dark past, he refuses to confess his love for her. However, when Winnifred gets well again and her doctor, Dr. Julian Harrow starts romancing her, Kev and Winnifred will soon realize that their love might be more powerful than any dark secret can hold back.<br /><br />Wow! I just have to say “wow” because this novel has totally blown me away with its dramatic writing and its brilliant title characters! Lisa Kleypas has definitely done a fantastic job at writing this novel about forbidden love and dark secrets and I thought that the “dark secrets” aspect of the story was woven into the story extremely well because it brought more drama to the story and it made the characters much more interesting to read about. What I really loved about this book were the characters themselves as they all have their dark secrets that they like to keep hidden from their loved ones, but they also know that if they keep those secrets hidden, they might risk losing the one they love. I really loved Winnifred Hathaway in this novel as she may seem weak because of her illness, but I started seeing a different side to her that I have never seen in the previous book and that was her determination to make Kev hers! Winnifred Hathaway has definitely shown so much courage and compassion for others in this book and that really made her stand out as a character that now she is on my list of favorite heroines and I really loved the way that she tries to help Kev open up his dark past to her because it showed how much she truly cared about him. Now, the hero of this story, Kev Merripen, is just awesome beyond all reason! At first, when I read “Mine Till Midnight,” he was shown to be always grumpy for no reason and it was a little hard for me to like his character. But, the moment I read this book, Kev Merripen is now officially one of my favorite romance heroes ever! I actually felt sorry for Kev whenever he had to come to grips with his dark past and how he was always worried about hurting Winnifred and that truly showed how caring and compassionate he really is despite his gruff nature. I also loved the mention of Kev’s massively muscular body since I love my romance heroes to be muscular and strong and Kev has got all the characteristics of a muscular and strong hero! I also loved seeing the continuing love of Cam and Amelia as it was just as dramatic in this story as it was in the previous book and I loved how Cam supported Kev throughout his trials of confessing his love towards Winnifred which truly made him into such a brilliant character and it was also great seeing Leo, the drunkard brother, regain his dignity in this book and he even helped out Kev with his relationship troubles. For romance fans, there are hot sizzling sexual scenes galore between Winnifred and Kev and they are just as steamy as Cam and Amelia’s and these scenes will make your romantic senses tingling as you read them!<br /><br />For those of you who do not like reading about sex scenes in a novel, this book has plenty of sex scenes between Winnifred and Kev, so it would be best to skim over these scenes if they are too uncomfortable to read through.<br /><br />Overall, “Seduce Me at Sunrise” is definitely a romance novel you cannot pass up and it is a brilliant sequel to the fantastic story “Mine till Midnight!” <br /><br /><b>Review is also on: <a href="http://rabbitearsbookblog.blogspot.com/2013/04/seduce-me-at-sunrise-by-lisa-kleypas.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Rabbit Ears Book Blog</a></b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15222096595506976151" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_24758833" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/24758833" />
    <a title="Daisiemae" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/838071-daisiemae"><img alt="Daisiemae" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1394577190p2/838071.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/24758833?book_show_action=true">Jun 17, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Daisiemae" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Daisiemae" href="/user/show/838071-daisiemae">Daisiemae</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">My friends who love a great romance.  Whew this was a great one!</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Daisiemae by: </span>
      <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.queuemyreview.com">www.queuemyreview.com</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/838071-daisiemae?shelf=series-romance">series-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/838071-daisiemae?shelf=books-to-i-will-never-part-with">books-to-i-will-never-part-with</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/838071-daisiemae?shelf=books-read-in-2008">books-read-in-2008</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/838071-daisiemae?shelf=historical">historical</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer24758833" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer883556744079569136">If I could give this book more than 5 stars I would.<br/>It has been years since I have read a Lisa Kleypas novel. I admittedly get stuck on a certain type of genre at times, and honestly stopped reading historical novels for a while. When I had the opportunity to read Seduce Me at Sunrise I jumped at the chance. Knowing that I have loved Lisa’s books in the past, I wondered if the magic was still there. It is. I had forgotten the lyrical way she tells a story. I forgot her addictive storylines and h</span>
  <span id="freeText883556744079569136" style="display:none">If I could give this book more than 5 stars I would.<br />It has been years since I have read a Lisa Kleypas novel. I admittedly get stuck on a certain type of genre at times, and honestly stopped reading historical novels for a while. When I had the opportunity to read Seduce Me at Sunrise I jumped at the chance. Knowing that I have loved Lisa’s books in the past, I wondered if the magic was still there. It is. I had forgotten the lyrical way she tells a story. I forgot her addictive storylines and her unbelievably tortured, sexy heroes…what was wrong with me? I am so glad I read this book. I simply loved every moment of it.<br /><br />Kevin Merripen has loved Winnifred Hathaway since they were kids. Abandoned by his gypsy clan, and rescued by the Hathaway’s he has always thought of himself not good enough for her, but he feels he must protect her from any pain and suffering that may come her way. Winnifred has always loved Kevin. Strong and silent, he gives her comfort with his quiet presence and fills her nights with unrequited longing. <br /><br />When Winn catches scarlet fever Kev is devastated. Afraid he might lose her, he nurses over her day and night. When her condition worsens, he remembers a remedy from his clan, and administers it to her. When Winn starts to recover, the bond between them grows even deeper. But, Winn has become weak from the fever and never fully recovers. Weak bodied, and not wanting Kev to settle on half a life with her, she knows she must do what she can to become healthier if she is ever to have Kevin’s love. When she hears about a Doctor that is practicing alternative medicine, this gives her hope to become better and be the woman she wants to be with Kev.<br /><br />Kev does not Winn to go. She is his light in the darkness he calls his life. After refusing his wishes for her to stay, he becomes ever more withdrawn and surly in her absence. As the years go by, Winn writes Kev, but he only writes her back once. Frustrated by Kev’s lack of communication she starts getting more involved with the handsome Doctor who helped her with her almost full recovery. When she arrives home, she is surprised by the dangerousness and loneliness that surrounds Kev. Even with the Doctor’s affection, Winn cannot forget the man she loves and the man she refuses to live without, so she decides to fight for him and what they can have together. <br /><br />What can I say about this book? Kev and Winn are a couple I loved to read about, I absolutely adored the Hathaway family! Not only is Seduce Me a Midnight the love story, but it is a story about survival and recovery from loss of loved ones and the determination it takes to have a happy life. Winn is a heroine that is smart, stubborn and knows how to fight to get her man. I can honestly say that most of the time I don’t like the heroines that I read about, but Winn is definitely a character that I cheered on and would like to call myself friends with. I cried with her, I cheered with her and I loved every romantic moment in this book. I truly hated for it to end, and I am anxiously awaiting the next book in this series. <br /><br />Seduce me at Sunrise can be read as a stand alone book. It is actually the second in the Hathaway series. Mine til Midnight is the first book in this series. Although, honestly I haven’t read Mine til Midnight yet, (I ordered it and will remedy that immediately), I had absolutely no trouble understanding the storyline and was able to follow along without any problems. <br /><br />Seduce Me at Sunrise has opened my eyes. Not only has it earned a coveted place on my crowded keeper shelf, I have re-discovered one of my favorite authors Lisa Kleypas. If you love a well told beautiful romance with a brooding, sexy hero and a super smart heroine, this book is for you! For more information on the Hathaway series and other books written by Lisa Kleypas, please visit her website at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.lisakleypas.com">www.lisakleypas.com</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="883556744079569136" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/88350974-somia?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/88350974-somia?shelf=5-sparkling-stars">5-sparkling-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/88350974-somia?shelf=lisa-kleypas">lisa-kleypas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/88350974-somia?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2584651462" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12729832434791897217">I forgot how good book 2 in the Hathaways series is, but this re-read has reminded me why I love LK’s HR books. <br/><br/>With Win Hathaway and Kev Merripen, Kleypas gives us a delicious historical romance, which is infused with heat, angst, tension and charm.<br/><br/>There’s a lovely intensity to the bond Merripen and Win share, one that ensures that despite Merripen’s stubbornness to not give in to his desires and yearning for Win to be his, since he feels she deserves better – we know he’ll sooner or later crac</span>
  <span id="freeText12729832434791897217" style="display:none">I forgot how good book 2 in the Hathaways series is, but this re-read has reminded me why I love LK’s HR books. <br /><br />With Win Hathaway and Kev Merripen, Kleypas gives us a delicious historical romance, which is infused with heat, angst, tension and charm.<br /><br />There’s a lovely intensity to the bond Merripen and Win share, one that ensures that despite Merripen’s stubbornness to not give in to his desires and yearning for Win to be his, since he feels she deserves better – we know he’ll sooner or later crack, after all he cannot be happy without her.<br /><br />Win's inner strength was fab to see, she never gives up and her threat to the doctor had me cheering her on. <br /><br />It was also a treat seeing all the Hathaways again, as well as seeing Cam, and the interactions between Marks and Leo had me grinning.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12729832434791897217" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_752645969" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/752645969" />
    <a title="Didi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6082482-didi"><img alt="Didi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459297426p2/6082482.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/752645969?book_show_action=true">Oct 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Didi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Didi" href="/user/show/6082482-didi">Didi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=angst-in-my-pants">angst-in-my-pants</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer752645969" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7571268983410135054">LOVED IT.<br/><br/>The second book in the Hathaways series was incredibly moving and somewhat somber. It was also much more angsty than LK's usual fare, and for that reason among many others, I loved it. It has earned a place on my forever favourites shelf.<br/><br/>Here, we get Merripen's( Kev ) and Winn's story. Having grown up with the Hathaways, Kev and Winn's enduring and complicated love was long overdue. Having Cam Rohan enter the fold and marry into her family, Winn decides she needs to improve her health i</span>
  <span id="freeText7571268983410135054" style="display:none">LOVED IT.<br /><br />The second book in the Hathaways series was incredibly moving and somewhat somber. It was also much more angsty than LK's usual fare, and for that reason among many others, I loved it. It has earned a place on my forever favourites shelf.<br /><br />Here, we get Merripen's( Kev ) and Winn's story. Having grown up with the Hathaways, Kev and Winn's enduring and complicated love was long overdue. Having Cam Rohan enter the fold and marry into her family, Winn decides she needs to improve her health if she is ever to move forward with Kev. But he doesn't want her to go, yet won't voice the longing and deep love he has for her. Winn is adamant though, hoping to finally bridge the gap between her and Kev, and put to rest her long-suffering condition, something which she feels stands in the way between them.<br /><br />A few years later, and everyone has changed: Winn for the better, Kev for the worst. Winn is much stronger, able to do things she could never do. And finally, FINALLY able to be the woman deserving of Kev. But he is not any more willing to succumb to his feelings and wants, more hardened to the belief that Winn deserves better.<br /><br />So he pushes her away. Repeatedly. It became stressful for me as a reader to experience what Winn felt every time she thought Kev was finally giving in. Only to be left alone, in doubt and questioning his feelings for her. But Kev was truly doing this to protect Winn. He sincerely believed that she deserved much better than what he could offer her. So it became a push-and-pull with them.<br /><br />I felt so bad for Winn. She was anguished and hurt beyond measure. The man she knew and loved just wouldn't give in to his feelings for her. But Kev was a tortured and suffering man. He was raised like a dog when he was with the Rom and never truly felt worthy of Winn's affections. His anguish was palpable. I felt so sorry for him and his torment over having to deny himself the one thing he truly wanted. I can't put it into words, but here's something he said to Winn that begins to explain his infinite love and desire for her:<br /><br />"All the fires of hell could burn for a thousand years and it wouldn't equal what I feel for you in one minute of the day. I love you so much there is no pleasure in it. Nothing but torment. Because if I could dilute what I feel for you to the millionth part, it would still be enough to kill you. And even if it drives me mad, I would rather see you live in the arms of that cold, soulless bastard than die in mine."<br />POWERFUL WORDS.<br /><br />And of course Kev is referring to the good Doctor Hallows, the man that helped Winn and now pursues her as a suitor. He was despicable and I was shocked to the lengths he went to to get what he wanted.<br /><br />But finally, Kev wakes up and sees his concerns are out of his hands. A veil is lifted off his eyes and he comes for Winn in the most beautifully savage and barbaric of ways, and I loved it!<br /><br />I loved seeing Cam Rohan again, that man is...WOW. He is so effortlessly charming, but in a subdued way, making it all the more alluring. And Leo. He came back with Winn, after being away for three years, a changed man. His dry wit and un-censored humour had me laughing out loud. At one point when speaking to Dr. Hallows, the bad doctor made a rude comment regarding Ms. Marks past, the governess hired to tutor Bea and Poppy. As he doesn't get along with her, Leo, in back handedly defending her honour, says:<br /><br />"I find that remark entirely inappropriate, It's obvious that no sane man would ever attempt something scandalous with Marks." <br />UNEXPECTED, BUT DRY HUMOUR!<br /><br />Leo has matured immensely after being away for years and it shows. He becomes a much more active member of the family and actually takes pleasure in tending to his household. At one point when confronting Kev over his self-destructive behaviour over Winn, he says:<br /><br />"Christ man, if you had the bullocks to die with her, don't you think you could work up the courage to live with her?"<br />LOVED THAT LINE.<br /><br />Needless to say, Lisa Kleypas is a literary genius. The only word to describe her written talent would be EVOCATIVE. I love losing myself in her world. Everything she writes has purpose, never any filler. Now I'm excited to read about Leo and Ms. Marks! <br /><br />LOVED THIS BOOK!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7571268983410135054" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_132050384" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/132050384" />
    <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352609417p2/2489554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/132050384?book_show_action=true">Nov 23, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Historical romance fans, especially girls who love their tortured hero</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog) by: </span>
      Lady Leah Westcliff
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-historical-romance">genre-historical-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=my-hottie-harem">my-hottie-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=king-of-the-harem">king-of-the-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=the-hymen-club">the-hymen-club</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=author-lisa-kleypas">author-lisa-kleypas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=covers-to-covet">covers-to-covet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=series-hathaways">series-hathaways</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=read-in-2011">read-in-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-go-rabid-over">books-i-go-rabid-over</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer132050384&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer132050384" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10952675724690118801"><b>Kev Merripen... gag me, tie me up and throw me over your shoulder! There is no need for you to kidnap me, I’ll come willingly!</b><br/><br/>I ADORE THIS BOOK! I am completely blown away by Kleypas’ writing in this one. It’s so lovely, so moving, and so sensual! I loved every moment of it! This will definitely be going on my keeper shelf, along with my other all-time favourites!<br/><br/>Win is such a likeable character. I enjoyed her fierceness and determined mindset despite the fact that she is physically weak in the </span>
  <span id="freeText10952675724690118801" style="display:none"><b>Kev Merripen... gag me, tie me up and throw me over your shoulder! There is no need for you to kidnap me, I’ll come willingly!</b><br /><br />I ADORE THIS BOOK! I am completely blown away by Kleypas’ writing in this one. It’s so lovely, so moving, and so sensual! I loved every moment of it! This will definitely be going on my keeper shelf, along with my other all-time favourites!<br /><br />Win is such a likeable character. I enjoyed her fierceness and determined mindset despite the fact that she is physically weak in the beginning. Because of her illness, others see her as weak and fragile, but emotionally, I think Win is just a strong as her sister Amelia. I love how the heroine is the one who knows exactly what she wants. She isn’t afraid to speak of her feelings towards Kev and let him know where she stands. <br /><br />Kev has become my favourite historical romance hero EVER! I adore this Rom completely. I love that we get to read about his past. Haunting as it is, I cannot help but fall more in love with him. It explains his quiet strength and his rawness. Kev is thorough in everything that he does. But he knows that because of his past and background, he puts Win under unnecessary scrutiny. There were times when I wanted to smack him because he’s so stubborn and determined not to be with Win, but after that moving confession by Leo about Laura, Kev finally fought for the right reasons.<br /><br />I loved his bitter confession of love to Win. It was so raw and revealing and completely passionate! As I said before, Kev is a by-the-book and thorough kind of guy. But his love for Win is soo irrational and out of control that when he does profess his love, it’s laced with torment and pain. He says, <b>“All the fires of hell could burn for a thousand years and it wouldn’t equal what I feel for you in one minute of the day. I love you so much there is no pleasure in it. Nothing but torment. Because if you could dilute what I feel for you to the millionth part, it would still be enough to kill you. And even if it drives me mad, I would rather see you live in the arms of that cold, soulless bastard than die in mine."</b><br /><br />Really, how is a girl supposed to respond to that? <br /><br />Speaking of that fucktard, Harrow I wanted to dice that bastard to pieces! How dare he try to poison Kev and as a result, poisoning Cam instead! I knew there was something terribly messed up with the guy but I didn’t expect something like this to occur. And the whole baby conceiving issue! Argh! I’m sooooooooooooo glad that Harrow was wrong about that! He probably said that because he can’t whip up the baby batter himself. That impotent ass!!!<br /><br />I also loved the bromance moments between Cam and Kev. Learning about thier link to one another was such a thrill to read. I also adore that moment when Leo spoke about his love, Laura. Moments like that make a girl melt, and I certainly swooned throughout this entire thing. <br /><br />I also have to mention that hilarious bickering and banter between Leo and Miss Marks! They are so entertaining together. That scene with Dodger the ferret and the vial was so hilarious. Leo is my man! Loved him!!!<br /><br /><b>Favourite Quote:</b><br />“Are you going to apologize, Merripen?”<br />Rohan twisted his arm a bit more tightly. “Do it, damn you,” Rohan muttered. “For the sake of the family.”<br />Glaring at the doctor, Kev spoke in Romany. “<i> Ka xlia ma pe tute</i>.” (I’m going to shit on you.)<br />“Which means, “ Rohan said hastily, “ ‘Please forgive the misunderstanding; let’s part as friends.’”<br />“<i> Te malavel les i menkiva</i>,” Kev added for good measure. (May you die of a malignant wasting disease.)<br />“Roughly translated,” Rohan said, “that means, ‘May your garden be filled with fine, fat hedgehogs.” Which, I may add, is considered quite a blessing among the Rom.”<br />Harrow looked skeptical. <br />Pg. 114<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10952675724690118801" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('CUy0nPUvBCHUqjSnuOPGflhY6GkYmFrnl9wIaWaW2wh87e/XS90tUyIbHcsEBuyxpziWgh5+jCAyap51om1TvA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
